Important News

Liu Shouzhong's Visit to Inner Mongolia 90

Meeting with the Panchen Lama to Encourage Education

Visiting Banner Kings to Inform Them to Focus on Defense

Suiyuan Correspondence - Liu Shouzhong, a member of the Central Committee of the Kuomintang, accompanied by secretaries Tan Chao-yi, Yang Jian-an, and Construction Director Feng Yi, Provincial Party Committee Zhao Yunyi, etc., departed from Suiyuan Province on the 13th to visit the Livelihood Canal, and to visit the Lama Cave in Bikqi. Those accompanied were also the 70th Division Commander Wang Jingguo, Finance Director Su Tiren, Jin-Sui Opium Suppression Inspection Office Director Li Juyi, and Provincial Government Secretary Gao Boyu. Zhang Xiusheng, the Superintendent of Saibei Customs. On the 14th, Liu also went to Bailing Temple with his secretary, Ji Shouguang, Gao Boyu, Zhang Jun, etc. to meet with the Panchen Lama, and then went to Maoming'an Banner, Daarhan Banner, and Siziwang Banner. After returning to the provincial city for a day of rest, he went to the five eastern counties to investigate. The details of his meeting with the Panchen Lama are recorded below:

Meeting with the Panchen Lama Bailing Temple is 450 li away from Suiyuan Provincial City. It was originally called Beile Wang Temple. Bailing is a corruption of Beile. Liu and his party took a car from the provincial city on the 14th and arrived at 6:20 PM, where they were received by Ding Wangduoji, the section chief of the Panchen Lama's office. Ding was a Tibetan. He sent a swift rider to report to the Panchen Lama. The Panchen Lama had originally planned to go to Zhonggong Banner to chant sutras early on the 15th and had already traveled dozens of li when the swift rider arrived and returned. Liu and his party arrived at White Stone Temple at 10:00 AM on the 15th. Wang Luojie, the Secretary-General of the Panchen Lama, and the Maoming'an Wang Banner Military Commissioner greeted them from afar, each presenting a [hada] (a long blue silk cloth of about two feet, the most respectful gift in Mongolia). At 11:00 AM, they met with the Panchen Lama, with Ding as the translator. Liu first said, "I have admired the great master for a long time, but I have had no chance to meet. I am very disappointed. The first time, the great master was in Beiping. I was eager to meet him, but the great master had already left first. The second time, the great master was visiting Wutai. I lived in Taiyuan and wanted to see him again, but because of matters involved, it was not possible. The third time, the great master was leaving Nanjing, and I arrived at the same time. We missed each other again. My desire to meet the great master is like Xuanzang of the Tang Dynasty seeking scriptures in India, going through many twists and turns (finally reaching the goal. Xuanzang was a Henan person, and his journey started from Chang'an. I am a Chang'an person, and my journey started from Luoyang. They are complementary to each other, which can be laughed at). The Panchen Lama was overjoyed to hear this, and then said, "I have long admired your Excellency's great name. I regret that we have missed many opportunities to meet. But Buddhism talks about karma. My meeting with your Excellency is probably destined and cannot be forced in the slightest. For example, if the fate of meeting each other is on March 3, but you want to meet on February 3 or April 3, it is impossible. Today, we meet in one hall, like brothers and sisters. How happy!" Liu continued, "At present, the Northeast has fallen, and Rehe is in emergency. National border defense is extremely important. Inner Mongolia is a northern screen, and its importance is self-evident. I hope that the great master will promote education in the various leagues and banners with a compassionate heart to save the world, increase the knowledge of the Mongolians, and prevent them from being bullied by strong neighbors." The Panchen Lama said, "I also know about this point. Please give me time, and I will promote it. When I visited the Eastern Provinces, I talked to the Eastern Province officials about how local officials often do not understand the Mongolian situation and abuse the Mongolians, so they harbor resentment. The central government gives preferential treatment to the Mongolians. I know this very well. This time, I will go to the Donggong, Zhonggong, and Xigong banners to chant sutras and, in addition to preaching Buddhism, I will declare the central government's intention to the public." After speaking, he personally unwrapped his watch and presented a fine horse, saying that the place was not peaceful, and he left it as a souvenir for those who came from afar. Then, they took a group photo and left.

Meeting with the Bailing King The Bailing Wang Mansion is also the Daarhan Wang Mansion, 90 li away from Bailing Temple. The Mongolian king of the banner also serves as the chief of the Ulanqab League. Recently, he let his younger brother manage the banner affairs. His younger brother is 53 years old, and the chief of the league is 58 years old. He spends all day chanting Buddha with his palms together. When Liu met with the Bailing King, after a brief greeting, the king first asked, "Is the mainland peaceful?" Liu told him that it was peaceful, and the king was very happy. Then he asked how the situation in Rehe was recently. Liu said, "Rehe is very dangerous. In recent years, the country has been plagued by many misfortunes and frequent foreign troubles. Inner Mongolia is an important border defense area of China. Once something happens, it will bear the brunt. I hope you will strive to be strong and continue the great cause of your ancestors. Don't just chant Buddha all day and be content with the status quo." The king said, "We have also been planning to consolidate border defenses for a long time, but we have repeatedly asked the government for guns and ammunition, but there has been no response. (According to people from the provincial government, the provincial government has given ammunition several times.) Even fools know that it is impossible to resist the enemy with bare hands. I sincerely ask the commissioner to say a word to the government to give us material assistance. Otherwise, if Inner Mongolia is in danger, I am afraid that the mainland will not be able to maintain itself for long." Liu also said, "The government has made up its mind to assist the Mongolian banners. If you do not work hard to revitalize yourselves, promote education, and cultivate the foundation, even if there is assistance, it will not be of long-term benefit. The central government is very concerned about the Mongolian banners. Many people will come to visit in the future. I am just a pioneer. I am determined to come again. I hope you will also go to the mainland." The king smiled and nodded, saying yes repeatedly. After the conversation, they took a group photo together as a souvenir.

What Was Seen in Maoming'an Banner Wang Luojie, the Secretary-General of the Panchen Lama's Office, introduced the younger brother of the Zhasake Military Commissioner of Maoming'an Banner (that is, the younger brother of the king of Zhonggong Banner) and more than ten people, including the military commissioner and Zuo Ling, to meet with Liu. They all wore red tassels and held the etiquette respectfully. In addition to the Panchen Lama's Office preparing the lunch on that day, the banner specially prepared a whole sheep to entertain the guests. When eating, a small piece was cut off with a knife and offered as a tribute. Then the honored guest ate the sheep's back, and the rest was cut and eaten by the guests at will. This is the most respectful etiquette of the Mongolians. The Living Buddha of Huangshitou Temple, 78 years old, was dignified. Liu and the Living Buddha and the Zhasake Vice League Chief and others took a group photo each, and then took a car back to Bailing Temple. The Panchen Lama also set off at the same time to Zhonggong Banner.

Meeting with Siziwang The Siziwang Mansion is 450 li away from the Bailing Wang Mansion. Sha Beizi traveled with him from Bailing Temple and stopped by his home to rest. He entertained the guests with milk tea, fried rice, milk cakes, etc. Along the way, only three or four yurts were seen. Surauli Temple, Tonghui Temple, Heto Temple, and Guangfu Temple are magnificent, embellishing the hundreds of miles of plain. When he arrived, it was already dark. The hosts were Military Commissioners, etc. Although the king had been ill for a hundred days and could not get up, when he heard that Liu had arrived, he sent someone to greet him and said that the king was currently ill and asked if the commissioner would like to see the king. Liu said that he had come specifically to visit the king's illness and then asked to see him. The king was lying naked on the bed, with only a single quilt covering his lower body, in a very sad state, saying that he would not be able to get up, but he was worried that his children were young and no one would take care of them. Liu comforted him kindly and promised to return to the provincial capital and ask the provincial government to hire a doctor on his behalf, and said, "Your position is important. You should take good care of yourself." The king was very moved when he heard this and nodded his head repeatedly. When Liu came out, there was a Military Commissioner who had assisted the king for three generations, 68 years old, energetic like a young man. Liu told him that the border defense was in emergency, and the Mongolians and the government were one and should cooperate to resist aggression. The Military Commissioner said, "Now that the five ethnic groups are united, the Mongolians seem to be an exception. What can we do to resist with empty fists?" While speaking, he pointed to the sky and said, "We can only resign ourselves to fate." Liu put his hands in a heart-shaped gesture and replied, "To resist foreign aggression, the first thing is to be united in mind and heart, and the material is secondary." The Military Commissioner nodded when he heard this and said yes repeatedly, and said that the Mongolians are strong, good at riding, and familiar with the terrain. In the event of an emergency, they will resist desperately and will never surrender under the city.

What Was Seen in Wulan Hua Wulan Hua is a large town in Wuchuan County, only 40 li away from the Siziwang Mansion. Before the traffic with Kulun was cut off, business was very prosperous. It is an important road connecting the mainland with Inner Mongolia. There are two former primary schools, one chamber of commerce, one district party headquarters, three or four collection agencies, and a garrison battalion commander Huang Shijun, who is very capable. He has concrete plans for repairing roads and running schools. Liu and Ji Shouguang of the Provincial Party Committee wanted to run a school in this town to recruit Mongolian children and cultivate real talents to develop the Northwest. It is currently under discussion.

Plans to Return to the Provincial City After Liu returned to the province, he immediately invited Construction Director Feng Xi, Civil Affairs Director Yuan Qingzeng, Provincial Government Secretary-General Zeng Houzai, Provincial Party Committee Ji Shouguang, Zhao Yunyi, and others to present their feelings about this trip to Mongolia and the guidelines for organizing the Mongolian banners and ask the provincial authorities to gradually realize them. The things to be done quickly at present are to run schools, unite the Mongolian banners, and organize Mongolian publications in the short term, and send a doctor to Siziwang Banner to treat the King of Siziwang. The trip cost 40 hours and passed through 2,000 li of grassland. At this time of emergency in border defense, Liu's trip has an impact on the communication between the mainland and the border, which is held up to inform the authorities responsible for organizing the Mongolian banners and those who are concerned about Mongolian affairs.

(Note) The official system of the Mongolian banners, each banner has a king. For the convenience of writing, the old name is also followed. (August 21st)

Engineers' Association Holds Annual Meeting in Tianjin 91

Famous Speakers All Hope to Save the Nation Through Science

Proposal to Join the Anti-Civil War Alliance Passed

Tianjin Correspondence: The second annual meeting of the Chinese Institute of Engineers was held at Nankai University on the morning of the 22nd of this month at 10:00 AM, with discussions in the afternoon regarding association affairs. Details are as follows:

The meeting hall was set up in Nanda’s Xiushan Hall. 127 members registered (82 from this city and 45 from other places). 120 people attended that day, with over 20 guests and journalists from various fields. Before the meeting, the giant bell of Nanda was rung twenty-one times, stopped for one minute, and then rung twice again to signify the 21st year of the Republic of China and the second general assembly. This bell was cast by the German Krupp factory when Li Hongzhang of the Qing Dynasty was the Minister of Beiyang, weighing 13,000 catties. It was initially placed in Haiguang Temple. After the Boxer Rebellion, the British moved it to a garden in the British concession until Zhang Boling negotiated for its return in the 19th year of the Republic of China. A bell tower was built on the Nanda campus to house it. The sound of the bell is grand and can be heard for dozens of miles, comparable to the bell of the Grand Bell Temple in the old capital. After the bell stopped, the meeting was opened with a ring, and rituals were performed. Hua Nan-gui, the temporary chairman, delivered an opening speech, stating that the association was formed last year by the merger of the Chinese Engineering Society and the Engineering Society of China. Before the merger, both associations had a history of 20 years. This is the second annual meeting after the merger. The association has over 2,000 registered members. Due to the current situation, very few people attended. The first meeting in Xi’an was changed to Tianjin due to inconvenient transportation. President Cao Yi-fu, who serves in the Ministry of Transportation, was unable to take leave to come to Tianjin due to the national crisis and asked me to represent him by telegram. Today, we are happy to gather here, and I hope that the attending members will express their great views and discuss them together. Engineers are laborers who are not afraid of hardship or difficulties. However, they should also connect and cooperate with all sectors to achieve twice the result with half the effort, thereby eliminating the accumulated habit of engineers not caring about national affairs. Finally, he said that engineers should have the construction courage of a tiger and the service spirit of a sheep, so that they can benefit the country. Next, Ji Shengfu Construction Department Chief Lin Chengxiu (representing Provincial Chairman Wang Shuchang) delivered a speech, stating that the country is now facing many difficulties and urgent foreign insults. The call for unity against aggression is very high, but the reality of unity against aggression is very difficult. Today, the unity of members of the Engineers' Association promotes construction. The annual meeting gathers to exchange knowledge. The responsibility of building a new China in the future will surely be the unanimous effort of your association, and the achievements in the future will be limitless. Next, Zhang Rui, Section Chief of the Municipal Government (representing Mayor Zhou Longguang), delivered a speech, stating that all countries regard the venue for scientific conferences as the highest honor. Today, the Chinese Engineering Society is holding a meeting in Tianjin, which is a great honor for the Tianjin Municipal Government. I still remember seven or eight years ago when Dr. Dewey came to China to give a lecture, among which a motto said, "China's affairs are too complicated, and it is difficult to make China rich and strong without a thousand good people." I feel that now that strong neighbors are oppressing and the foundation of the country is shaking, it is no longer possible for good people who talk about morality and benevolence to save China. At least five hundred of the thousand good people must be engineers to respond to the environment and create a new life. All of you members are either engineering experts or engineering celebrities. I hope that you will serve the society with a spirit of perseverance and build a new China. Once again, Zhang Boling, President of Nanda University, delivered a speech, first expressing his welcome as the host. Then he stated that since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have been very uncomfortable, but it is actually an excellent opportunity to save the country, which can give a serious lesson to those who are drunk and dreaming. China's problem lies in talking empty talk and not doing practical things. During the Yuan Shikai era, training troops and developing schools were regarded as two major policies to strengthen the country, but now they have become two major diseases of the country. Japan's strength comes from science, so people with ideas should not speak out when they are bullied, but should work hard to prepare for resistance, otherwise they will undoubtedly die. China is sick because of poverty and weakness. The wealth and strength of Europe and the United States come from science. They can use it, but why can't we? Your spirits and brains are no weaker than those of Westerners, and even the Japanese are not as good as us. Why is our country still poor and weak? The reason is that politics is not on track. Not only can national affairs not be handled, but private businesses are also often hindered. When you were studying in Europe and the United States, your aspirations and ambitions were met with obstacles everywhere after returning to China, causing heroes to have no place to use their talents. I have vowed to run education as a lifelong career for decades, and I don't care about national affairs. In recent years, I have begun to feel that the political is bad, and all citizens cannot but care about it. The annual meeting of the Engineers' Association is of great significance. Unity and cooperation can generate great power. However, you must not remain silent on national affairs, and change your previous attitude of not minding your own business, so that politics can be on track and everything can be easily started. Therefore, I deeply hope that you can have practical and concrete expressions, cheer up, and find a new life for our country. If the spirit is bankrupt, the country will surely perish. Your responsibilities are extremely important, and the hope of the country lies in this. Once again, Fan Xudong, the founder of Yongli Chemical Company, gave a speech entitled "Ancient Engineering Creation and Modern Engineering Performance," talking about the Stone Age to the Scientific Age, in thousands of words. It was the most colorful and moving speech on that day. Next, Bian Baimei, the representative of the Bankers' Association, delivered a speech, saying that the situation is unstable, foreign insults are pressing, and aggression is becoming increasingly urgent. Not only are there military occupations, but all industrial and commercial undertakings are being invaded. Since the September 18th Incident, traffic and shipping routes have been repeatedly obstructed. All of these are within the scope of engineers' work. We should strive to study new constructions and create new life, even if we sacrifice everything, to develop a major expansion and provide assistance in military and political aspects, which can achieve final victory. Furthermore, the Haihe River problem is of great importance to the industry, commerce, and agriculture of North China. I hope to point out the mistakes from a fair and scientific perspective and correct them. If funds are needed, the financial community will naturally help. Tianjin's industry is not developed. Regarding the establishment of factory organizations, I hope to publish fair opinions and guidance so that the financial community can know the truth and jointly develop it. Next, Wang Wendian, the representative of the Chamber of Commerce, delivered a speech, stating that to know the prosperity or decline of industry and commerce in a certain place, you can look at the number of chimneys in that place and the comparison of import and export goods at the customs. The increase in chimneys in major commercial ports in our country is very slow, and the customs revenue far exceeds exports. Our country's poverty is due to poor politics, but the decline of social customs and habits is also a major reason. If there is no way to deal with the two things I said, even if there are 20,000 engineers, it will be useless. Therefore, everyone should stand up and work together to save the country. Finally, Zhang Hanying, the representative of the Jinan branch of the Engineering Society, delivered a congratulatory speech, and Hua Nankui delivered a thank-you speech. Then, a group photo was taken and the meeting adjourned. The Tianjin branch of the Engineering Society hosted a banquet at the Nanda Canteen to welcome everyone.

From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM, the first business meeting was held, chaired by Mao Yisheng. First, Zhang Xiaoji, the representative of the General Assembly, reported on the association's work in the 20th year and the association's regular income and expenditure in the same year. Then, Zhang Hanying reported on the work of the Jinan branch. Hua Nankui reported on the receipt of the files of the Beiping Chinese Engineers Association Housing Case. Next, more than ten proposals on the association's affairs were passed, and a case to join the Great Alliance to Abolish Internal Wars was passed. By the time the meeting adjourned, the sun had set in the west. Zhang Boling prepared tea and snacks on the roof of the Nanda Mu Zhai Library to entertain everyone. The wives of the school's faculty members all served as hosts. At 7:00 PM, they took cars to the Yong'an Hotel to attend a banquet hosted by the provincial government. The heads of the provincial civil affairs, finance, education, and construction departments all attended to receive them. Wang Yuke, the head of the Civil Affairs Department, delivered a welcome speech, briefly stating that China now needs construction, and engineers have risen to the first position in society. The Soviet Union's five-year plan is an engineering plan, so Chinese engineers should seize the opportunity to work hard. Two thousand members is not a small number, but it cannot be said to be many when measured against the national population. I hope that the Engineering Society will be the foundation for building a prosperous and strong Republic of China. In this way, there is hope for construction. Today, I would like to offer a glass of water and wine to congratulate all members on their success, the progress of the Chinese Engineers Association, and the bright future of the Republic of China. Hua Shanggui then delivered a thank-you speech on behalf of the group. At 8:30 PM, the guests and hosts all enjoyed themselves and dispersed. (Evening of August 22nd)

Mathematics and Physics Society Holds Annual Meeting in Beiping 92

Six Papers Read

Beiping Correspondence: The Chinese Society of Mathematics and Physics held its third annual meeting in Beiping City starting on the 22nd, and held public lectures. Meetings continued on the 23rd and 24th. Details are as follows: At 9:00 AM on the 22nd, a public lecture was held in the Second College of Peking University. Gu Cheng of the Women's College gave a lecture on "What is a Curve." More than 100 people attended. Gu's arguments were detailed, and the meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. At 12:00 noon, the members in Beiping held a public banquet for the members who came to Beiping in the waterside pavilion of Zhongshan Park. More than 30 people, including Li Shuhua, attended. During the banquet, the president, Ma Zuxun, first reported that many members came to Beiping to attend this annual meeting, and the Ministry of Education did not send a special representative to attend, etc. Afterwards, Chen Kezhong, the representative of the Ministry of Education, explained the Ministry of Education's expectations for the Chinese Society of Mathematics and Physics, and then Xia Yuanchen, Huang Jiyu, Sun Guofeng, etc., delivered speeches.

The banquet adjourned at 2:00 PM. At 3:00 PM, the third annual meeting was held in the waterside pavilion of Zhongshan Park. More than 30 members attended. After the meeting, President Feng Zuxun first reported on the association's work in the previous year. Then, Vice President Zhang Yihui chaired the meeting and discussed the following proposals: (1) The case of reviewing and determining the names of mathematical and physical terms was resolved to organize a translation name committee for mathematics and physics, with five committee members in the mathematics group and five committee members in the physics group. (2) The standard case of mathematics and physics courses was resolved to organize a middle and primary school curriculum committee, with five committee members in each of the mathematics and physics groups. (3) The case of the association's publications was resolved to be handled by the council. (4) A telegram to congratulate the World Society of Mathematics and Physics was resolved to be passed and a telegram was sent to Tai Qingfeng, a member of the association, to represent the association at the Swiss International Mathematical Conference. (5) The case of members of the association visiting scenic spots was resolved to be freely combined by members and then elect staff. The meeting adjourned at about 7:00 PM.

In addition, the meeting schedule for the 23rd of the association was to visit from 9:00 AM and hold a committee meeting at 1:00 PM, which was held at Tsinghua University. They stayed at Tsinghua University that night. The meeting schedule for the 24th was to give papers at Tsinghua University from 9:00 AM and attend the Tsinghua University reception at noon. A total of six papers were read: (1) Feng Hanshu's paper [Cauchy's Integral Theorem] (2) Huang Renchu's paper [A Certain Theorem of Definite Integral and a Study of a Certain Indefinite Integral] (3) Fan Bingjun's paper [A Class of Several Exceptional Meromorphic Functions] (4) Zhang Yufeng's paper [Vector Analysis] (5) Jiang Zehan's paper [Branch Points of Harmonic Functions and Colin's Functions in the Plane] (6) Zhao Xisan's paper [Asymptotic Values of Entire Functions I. (23rd)]

Zhenjiang Abolishes the Erqi Bao Silver Standard 93

Decision to Implement from the End of This Year

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Commerce submitted a request to abolish taels and change to yuan, the Department of Industry has published a proposal to abolish taels and change to yuan. The Zhenjiang County Party and government organs believe that the Zhenjiang Erqi Bao silver standard hinders commercial development and that it is necessary to abolish it first. After discussion and decision by the Party and government talks, the silver industry and experts were invited to organize a discussion on the abolition of the Erqi Bao. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the discussion held its first meeting in the Chamber of Commerce Building. The attendees were Hu Jianchun, Li Songshan, Cai Yunsu, Hu Jingxuan, Qian Pengxian, Yan Junfu, Lu Xiaobo, Zhang Peng, Wu Tixian, Yu Xiaochuan, Yao Qisu, Wang Zhao Jia, Zhang Yisun, Yang Fangzhen, Yu Yinxuan, (Zhu Qingquan's representative). Zhang Peng was the chairman. The meeting opened as usual. First, the chairman and Yao Qisu, the county committee member, reported on the significance of organizing the discussion. Then, Li Songshan, Lu Xiaobo, Yang Fangzhen, Wu Tixian, Hu Jianchun, Hu Jingxuan, Yan Junfu, etc., expressed their opinions, which can be summarized into two types: One is that although abolishing the Erqi Bao silver standard is a must, there should be a meticulous plan before it is abolished, otherwise it will affect the development of industry and commerce and the social economy. It may fall into the same fate as the bankruptcy of Hankou and Changsha. We must take precautions. Shanghai is the financial hub of the country. Now that Shanghai is proceeding with abolishing taels and changing to yuan, Zhenjiang may as well use Shanghai as the basis. One is that after Zhenjiang abolishes the Erqi Bao, industry and commerce can avoid suffering losses from foreign currency besides profit and loss. The Erqi Bao no longer has spot goods and is a kind of fictitious silver standard. After the abolition, there will be no difficulties. The economic chaos in Hankou, Changsha, and other places in the past was not caused by the abolition of taels and changing to yuan, but for other reasons. Finally, it was decided that (1) Zhenjiang's Erqi Bao silver standard will be abolished after the end of this year's business community. (2) The discount standard will be negotiated and determined by the Chamber of Commerce to convene the money industry and all industries. (3) Contribute opinions to the national abolition of taels and change to yuan. (25th)

Because of gambling, he was dismissed and returned home. The Suicide of a Military Officer's Wife. The wife of a certain military officer in Yongbu, Ms. Liang, is 22 years old this year and studied at a girls' school. She is of excellent character and learning. Ms. Liang was betrothed to a certain military officer by her parents when she was two years old. They got married and lived together in February of this year. However, Ms. Liang has been frowning all day since she got married, and she is always depressed, as if she has unspeakable secrets, causing her to suffer from lung disease. On the 8th of this month, she was admitted to the North Gate Renze Hospital for treatment and lived in Room 14 of the female doctor's office. A certain military officer must visit once a day. As soon as his wife saw him, she sobbed and said nothing. On the afternoon of the 19th, she suddenly asked the doctor for an hour's leave, saying that she was going out to visit a friend. She went to the North Gate Ferry to commit suicide by throwing herself into the river. Did Ms. Liang become tired of the world because of her illness, or is there another secret? Outsiders do not know.

Education News

Important News: Luo Jialun Firmly Resigns from President of National Central University 106

A telegram from Nanjing on the 25th states that Luo Jialun received the government's order appointing him as President of National Central University on the 25th. He immediately submitted his resignation and made a statement to reporters, saying, "When the Executive Yuan decided to appoint me as President of National Central University, I told reporters that I would submit my resignation as soon as the order arrived. Now that I have received the order, I am submitting my resignation immediately. My intention to resign is very firm. In recent years, I have been tired of educational administration. After a major resignation in the past, I retreated to Wuhan University as a professor. Later, the central authorities urged me to return to Chang Central Political School because I had participated in the founding of the school and had emotional ties in addition to a sense of duty. I could not bear to refuse. After arriving at the school, I set a goal to make the school like the French political school. The national crisis suddenly broke out, and I encouraged the youth day and night to take on the responsibility of the French political school after the Franco-Prussian War, to reform domestic politics as the basis for wiping out shame and striving for strength. Fortunately, the whole school is working hard and all reforms are underway. I will never abandon it to engage in the ever-increasing storms and the hundreds of things that need to be managed at National Central University. I and the entire political school will share the hardships for nearly a year. Leaving it to go elsewhere would not only be unfair to my colleagues at the political school, but also to the young students. Although the government intends for me to concurrently hold a position at the political school, I believe that responsibility should be dedicated and not concurrent, lest it lead to errors. I am confident that the government will surely heed my wishes. Recent reports of my remarks, stating that the government did not seek my consent beforehand, are absolutely not true. I only said that I repeatedly subtly agreed, but I have never dared to agree to this day. It is also said that I am too ill to bear the burden. I have indeed been ill recently, but it has nothing to do with my resignation from National Central University. Although I am ill, I absolutely do not want to consider myself an invalid. I have always been very straightforward in my work and would never want to use illness as an excuse for shirking responsibility," etc. (Central News Agency)

The Annual Meeting of the Society for Social Education Opens in Hangzhou 107

The Ceremony Was Held in the Morning: A General Meeting Continued in the Afternoon

The first annual meeting of the China Society for Social Education opened yesterday (the 24th) at 9:00 AM at the Zhejiang Provincial Library on Puzhang Lane in Hangzhou. Attendees included Yang Donglin, representative of the Central Party Headquarters; Peng Baichuan, representative of the Ministry of Education; Hu Jianzhong, representative of the Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters; Qian Jiazhi, representative of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education; Zhong Daozan, representative of the Fujian Provincial Department of Education; Xiang Jutan, representative of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education; and members Yu Qingtang, Shu Xincheng, Shang Zhongyi, and more than eighty others. Zheng Zonghai served as chairman, and Zhao Guangtao and Li Bangquan served as recorders. After the formalities were completed, the chairman delivered the opening address, stating that the society was just over a year old, but social education activities had been with people since birth. From childhood to adulthood, people are constantly receiving education, but in the past, Chinese etiquette and education mostly focused on subtle influence, touching people unconsciously. The times have evolved, and intangible social education has evolved into tangible education that supplements knowledge and enhances skills. Social education establishes various activity organizations, such as public education centers and libraries, which are tangible and concrete manifestations. The target of social education, in a broad sense, is all our Chinese compatriots, including farmers, workers, merchants, students, soldiers, men, women, old, and young, all of whom are receiving education. Since the quality is so complex and the quantity is so large, it is not easy to achieve the greatest effect in a very short time, with very little money, and with very few people. Furthermore, in terms of the current national situation, the century-long plan for cultivating talents is indeed important, but it is not enough to meet the urgent needs, and there is also the fear of the nest overturning and the eggs being broken. Therefore, today, in order to seek emergency relief, it is necessary to carry out horizontal and universal propaganda among the people, and it is also necessary to start with popular education. The members of this society feel that social education is an urgent and needed cause, and they also feel the importance of this mission. For all facilities, theories, and practices of social education, there is a need for collective consultation and discussion. Therefore, this society was initiated, and today's annual meeting is being held. The content of this meeting can be divided into four categories: (1) social education and education system issues, (2) rural improvement issues, (3) improving research interest and methods, and (4) exchange of popular reading materials and other publications. In addition, each service organization reports on its work for mutual reference, and the most important topic is still the effectiveness, estimation, and statistical methods of adult education, in order to determine the final education

standards. This is also the central issue of this annual meeting. After the chairman's speech, Yu Qingtang, director of the board of directors' office, reported on the general situation of the office's work. Then, Yang Donglin, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, and Peng Baichuan, representative of the Ministry of Education, delivered training speeches. Hu Jianzhong, representative of the Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters, and Qian Jiazhi, Zhong Daozan, and Xiang Jutan, representatives of the education departments of various provinces, delivered speeches successively. Then, members Ma Zongrong and Dong Huaihuangzhong delivered speeches in succession. The general meeting was held at 2:00 PM, chaired by Gao Yang, chairman of the presidium, to discuss all the proposals. Because the total number of proposals exceeded seventy, special review committee members were elected. As a result, Yu Qingtang, Gan Yuyuan, Zhao Mian, Shu Xincheng, Ma Zongrong Gao Yang, Zheng Zonghai, Xiang Jutan, Peng Baichuan, Dong Huai, Shang Zhongyi, and Zhong Daozan were selected as review committee members. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM, followed by a review meeting, which was divided into four categories: special, administrative, facilities, and social affairs, which were submitted for review. It was not completed until 7:00 PM.

Revised Standards for Primary School Curriculum 108

The decisions of the Curriculum Standards Revision Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools regarding the curriculum for junior high schools and senior high schools have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. (As a temporary motion, there is also the issue of whether junior high schools and senior high schools should have co-education or whether boys and girls should be taught in separate classes. Because the case is important and cannot be decided in a short time, it will be decided by the Ministry of Education. Also, the case of whether junior high school teachers' salaries should stop being based on the hourly system will be sent to the Ministry of Education for reference because the Ministry of Education will soon stipulate measures for teachers' salaries.) The resolution on the primary school curriculum has also been slightly revised after being sorted out by the responsible department of the Ministry of Education. The following is a summary of the various resolutions, compiled as follows: (Those comprehensive resolutions that have not yet been determined or have only been initially determined and cannot be officially announced are recorded in a slightly simplified manner.)

(Zi) During the meeting, the attending committee members were divided into several groups to revise the content and writing style of the original primary school curriculum standards, and to separately designate revision committee members for each subject, including health, music, Chinese, kindergarten, arithmetic, social studies, nature, physical education, art, and manual labor.

(Chou) After the formal promulgation of the curriculum standards, the Ministry of Education is requested to devise ways to create standards for testing various subjects in primary schools as the basis for concrete graduation standards for various subjects in primary schools.

(Yin) In the general outline of the primary school curriculum standards, except for the first item [General Objectives of Primary School Education], which was largely revised during the first day of the meeting (as reported in the previous newspaper) and was reviewed again during the fifth meeting, the original draft was used without revision. The full text of the original draft is as follows: [First] General Objectives of Primary School Education] Primary schools should, in accordance with the party's program, follow the educational purpose of the Republic of China and its implementation policies, implement child-centered education to develop children's physical and mental health, cultivate the foundation of national morality, and the basic knowledge and skills necessary for life. The analysis is as follows: 1. To train children's healthy physique; 2. To cultivate children's good character; 3. To develop children's life skills; 4. To train children's labor skills; 5. To cultivate children's scientific attitude; 6. To increase children's artistic interests.) The rest will be sorted out by the standing committee.

(Mao) Revise the outline of the curriculum standards. (The content is not yet convenient to publish) (Chen) A table should be established in the general outline of the implementation methods of this standard to indicate the books used for each subject (to be determined by the standing committee).

(Ji) The positions of the general principles of teaching and the implementation methods in the general outline should be reversed. (Wu) No party ideology course is set up. All civic knowledge is incorporated into the social studies teaching, and civic training is added, with sixty minutes per week.) Therefore, the social studies score for senior grades is increased, with one hundred and eighty minutes per week, nature one hundred and fifty minutes, and art increased by thirty minutes to a total of ninety minutes. There are no significant changes in other subjects.

(Wei) Resolutions on various issues related to civic training:

(1) When increasing the standards for civic training and recommending members to draft and compile, attention should be paid to:

1. The purpose of civic training is to train character and behavior. 2. Two sessions should be scheduled on the overall timetable each week as guidance time (etiquette, practices, and behavioral practice). 3. Use group activities as opportunities for civic training. 4. In addition to the class teacher or instructor being responsible for special training, all other teachers in the school must be responsible for training. 5. The main points of the training method should explain that textbooks are not allowed and only teaching methods for teachers can be compiled. 6. Civic training should guide children with concrete standards, using pictures, music, stories, etc., and implement it practically.

(2) Compile an outline of the civic training curriculum: 1. Objectives, 2. Concrete standards (concrete standards are compiled by year and summarized into several programs), 3. Key points of the training method.

The final meeting reviewed the operational points of civic training and determined four major categories: 1. Regarding morality, 2. Regarding recreation, 3. Regarding politics, 4. Regarding economics.

(3) Determine the objectives of civic training: 1. To cultivate children's noble character and good behavior; 2. To cultivate children's strong physique and happy emotions; 3. To cultivate children's ability to organize groups and the spirit of social service; 4. To develop children's labor habits and interest in production.

(4) This group's meeting will formulate the main points of the civic training method and hand them over to the standing committee to determine the training method (main points attached).

(5) The standing committee will sort out and classify the detailed items of civic training based on existing materials, establish a table by year, and send it to the members of this group for a limited time to report their opinions before making a decision (the content of the table should include at least: 1. Articles, 2. Whether or not it is necessary, 3. Category, 4. Grade system).

(Shen) The curriculum standards for health, art, music, kindergarten, and other subjects were passed in accordance with the review plan amendment. The standards for Chinese, nature, manual labor, physical education, arithmetic, and other subjects were passed in accordance with the revision opinions.

(You) The middle school group suggested that attention be paid to the connection between the curriculum of primary and secondary schools and the functions of primary and junior high schools. The resolution was to formulate opinions and send members to the middle school group for explanation. Suggested content (Chinese language): 1. In principle, junior high school students should use vernacular Chinese for written expression. 2. When teaching classical Chinese at the beginning of junior high school, the amount should be reduced as much as possible to maintain the originally set ratio of classical Chinese to vernacular Chinese (arithmetic): The level of arithmetic in primary schools has been lowered. It is hoped that the level of arithmetic in junior high schools will be lowered by one year compared with the past in order to connect (general opinion) (1) During primary school education (in accordance with the stipulated school system), children cannot decide on their future careers. This responsibility should be borne by junior high schools. It is hoped that in the future, the junior high school curriculum should still have the function of exploring children's vocational interests and should not be limited to entering higher education (2) The Ministry of Education has previously issued an order that all subjects in junior high school, except for Chinese language, which can be used in classical Chinese, should generally be used in vernacular Chinese. Please pay attention to this.

Rural Educator Tu Xian Passes Away 110

Rural educator Tu Xianjun, a native of Suichang, Zhejiang, graduated from the College of Education of Great China University. He successively served as a teacher at Shanghai Peiming Girls' Middle School, director of the library of Shanghai Provincial Middle School, lecturer at Southeast Women's Physical Education School, and director of the Xianghu Rural Normal Education School of Zhejiang Province. He was enthusiastic in his work and was determined to improve rural education. He died of overwork and illness, and all medicines were ineffective. He unfortunately died at 4:10 AM yesterday morning (the 25th) at the Shanghai Hospital in Nanshi. Tu Jun's teachers, friends, and acquaintances were all extremely saddened by the news, and they especially lamented the loss of talent for the future of rural education.

Vocational Education Society Raises Salaries to Help the Righteous Army 111

The colleagues of the China Vocational Education Society believe that the atmosphere of the northeastern bandits is becoming increasingly urgent, and all the righteous armies rely on hand-to-hand combat to fight hard, still delaying a ray of hope. Although all circles in this city and overseas Chinese have given material assistance, temporary fundraising cannot help in long-term resistance. Therefore, at the 455th staff meeting of the society the other day, it was decided that from this month onwards, all staff and members of the society would donate 2% of their monthly salaries until the day the righteous army succeeds in resisting Japan. In addition, all affiliated organizations were notified to refer to and imitate it. Although this move by the society is not large in number, its intention is far-reaching. If all agencies can imitate it, then although it is a drop in the bucket, the righteous army should have a relatively permanent source of funds. It is thought that patriotic gentlemen at home and abroad will be able to rise up in response to the news.

Chinese Women's Physical Education Normal School Establishes an Attached Elementary School 114

The attached elementary school of the Chinese Women's Physical Education Normal School was originally located on Qingyun Road, Zhabei. After the Shanghai Incident occurred and the school building was burned down, it moved to Julai Da Road in the French Concession with the normal school department to continue its operation. It opened on the 20th, and many new students have reported. It is now scheduled to start classes on the 25th. It is heard that there are still vacancies in each grade. Nearby students can go to register as soon as possible. In addition, the normal school department is scheduled to open on September 1st.

Cai Tingkai Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 128

Accompanied by Aide-de-Camp Tang Dehuang

Staying at Song's Residence, Heading to the Capital Today or Tomorrow

Cai Denies Chen Mingshu's Taking Over Fujian

General Cai Tingkai, Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army and Acting Pacification Commissioner of Fujian Province, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 8:00 AM on the Dutch ship "Chisalia" from Xiamen. He immediately visited Song Ziwen, Chen Mingshu, Dai Ji, and others, and plans to go to the capital within the next few days to report to the central government on the recent situation of bandit suppression. The following is a detailed account of Cai's arrival in Shanghai and his remarks:

Arrival in Shanghai: Cai Tingkai, accompanied by Tang Dehuang, Director of the Aide-de-Camp Office, and Aide-de-Camp Ye Lixin, arrived in Shanghai on the Dutch ship "Chisalia" from Xiamen on the 22nd of this month. The ship encountered a storm en route, delaying its arrival at Wusong Estuary until 5:00 AM yesterday. It reached the Yitaixing Wharf in Pudong at 6:30 AM. Due to the strong wind and rapid currents, the ship had difficulty turning around, which took a long time. Therefore, Cai did not wait for the ship to dock and instead boarded the Hai Guan Jinghui patrol boat that came to meet him. He landed at the New Customs Wharf at 7:40 AM.

Welcoming Party: Those who boarded the Dutch ship on the Jinghui patrol boat yesterday morning to welcome Cai included Fan Qiwu, former Director of the Rear Affairs Office of the 19th Route Army (the rumor that Fan came with Cai is incorrect, as Fan has been in Shanghai all along, residing at the Cangzhou Hotel), Wang Zhiyuan, Manager of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, Lin Jin, representative of Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji, Tang Haian, representative of Song Ziwen, Lu Wenlan, Salt Transport Commissioner of Songjiang, and more than a dozen of Cai's relatives and friends.

Visiting Song and Meeting Chen: After landing, Cai, accompanied by Fan Qiwu, Tang Haian, and others, took a car to Song's residence on Qiqi Road to visit Song Ziwen. They talked until 9:40 AM. Cai then went to Shanzhong Road with Fan Qiwu to meet with Chen Mingshu, talking for an hour. At 11:00 AM, he returned to Song's residence, where Song Ziwen hosted a welcome banquet. At 4:30 PM, Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji went to Song's residence to meet with Cai. Around 6:00 PM, they went out together. Cai stayed overnight at Song's residence. Tang Dehuang and others who came with him were taken to the Longhua Headquarters by Lin Jin, Director of the Aide-de-Camp Office of the Garrison Command, to meet with Commander Dai and report on everything.

Heading to the Capital Soon: According to reliable sources, in addition to reporting on the military affairs of bandit suppression to the central government and discussing financial issues, Cai's visit also involves important matters to be negotiated with Chen Mingshu. Cai will be going to the capital today or tomorrow, possibly traveling by Sikorsky plane with Song Ziwen. As for the date of his return to Fujian, it is expected to be in about two weeks.

Cai's Remarks: Cai met with reporters from various newspapers at Song's residence yesterday morning, saying, "The purpose of my trip north is to report on the bandit suppression work to the central government, so my stay in Shanghai will be very short. Because I have been apart from Minister Song and Minister Chen for many days, I went to visit them immediately after getting off the ship for a brief chat. My visit to Song was not to discuss financial issues in Fujian. Chairman Fang Taosheng is responsible for the finances of Fujian Province, and I am only offering my assistance in terms of friendship. Recently, there have been rumors that the Fujian provincial government is about to be reorganized and that Chen Mingshu will go to Fujian to take charge. These are all rumors. As for the bandit situation in Fujian, since our army launched the suppression campaign, the main force of the bandits has retreated to the Longyan area in western Fujian. The front line of the bandit suppression army is about thirty miles away from Longyan, consisting of the 61st Division and a part of the 78th Division. However, there are still scattered bandits roaming around, but they can be quickly wiped out once pursued. Tan Qixiu's supplementary brigade has now arrived and is stationed in Fuzhou. The bandit suppression work is still actively underway. The reports that the Guangdong army suddenly withdrew from southern Fujian are completely untrue. Opium seedlings are everywhere in Fujian Province, and the opium ban has been relaxed. After our army arrived in the province, we immediately ordered the ban on opium. Anyone who smokes or grows opium will be severely punished once arrested, so opium cultivation is about to disappear, but very few smokers have quit. I deeply hope to eradicate opium in Fujian Province in the shortest possible time." The reporter then asked about his attitude towards the Japanese army's repeated invasion of Rehe and the crisis in the Northeast. Cai was quite indignant upon hearing this, saying that he deeply regrets the fall of the Northeast and that it is even more painful to think about when the lost territory will be recovered. He hopes that everyone, from top to bottom, will be united and determined to resist foreign aggression, so that there will be a day to avenge our humiliation and strengthen our country.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Protect Overseas Merchants 129

Urges Careful Selection of Consular Personnel and Strict Performance Evaluation

Recommends Dispatching Warships to Patrol and Protect Compatriots

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that overseas merchants in various places have been subjected to destruction by local governments in recent years, leading to a miserable situation abroad. Yesterday, it sent a special cable to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that overseas consuls be instructed to strive for protection and that warships be dispatched to patrol and protect overseas Chinese. The original cable is recorded as follows: "To the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing: Overseas Chinese residing abroad are mostly laborers and vendors selling local products needed by overseas Chinese. This is not enough to be considered international commerce. Recently, with the domestic new industries taking shape, these products have been exported to some extent, deeply provoking the jealousy of local industrialists and merchants, who have resorted to all kinds of destructive measures. Recently, the prohibition of the sale of Apollo light bulbs in Batavia, and the prohibition of the import of Yonghe Industrial Company's cosmetics by a certain commercial bank in Burma two years ago, are just a few examples that are chilling. Consuls are originally commercial affairs officials and have the responsibility to protect the merchants of their own country. The above-mentioned places are not without our country's consuls stationed there, but their efforts to mediate have not been effective at all. They are derelict in their duties and cannot escape public criticism. We urge your ministry to be extra cautious in the selection of overseas consular personnel and to raise adequate funds to avoid the frequent lack of funds for consulates. Then, strict performance evaluations should be established, with the promotion and demotion of each consul determined by the effectiveness of their protection, so that overseas commerce can gradually progress. The country would be fortunate. Moreover, even after the destruction of the navy in the late Qing Dynasty, there were still instances of dispatching warships to comfort overseas Chinese, which had a positive impact on international perception and the protection of overseas Chinese. In recent years, since the massacre of overseas Chinese in Korea, this practice has almost disappeared, except for the dispatch of a Zhenhai warship to comfort the victims in the Northeast after the incident. This has made overseas Chinese feel even more abandoned by their motherland. We urge your ministry to submit a proposal to the Executive Yuan, which should be put on the agenda, requiring the Ministry of the Navy to select warships from the First Fleet each year that are capable of sailing overseas for patrols, establishing connections with foreign countries while implicitly protecting overseas Chinese. This seems to be the most important task today. We hope you will consider and handle this matter appropriately. Respectfully, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Lu Lu, Captain of the Police Brigade, Left Shanghai Yesterday with Peace Police 134

Heading Back to Peace via Jinpu Railway

Since the January 28th Incident, the police force in the war zone has been weak. Therefore, Mayor Wu transferred a police brigade from Peiping, led by Captain Lu Lu, to Shanghai to assist the Municipal Public Security Bureau in maintaining security in northern Shanghai. At that time, it coincided with the signing of the ceasefire agreement, and the Japanese troops gradually withdrew. A large number of Peiping police were transferred to Zhenru and Zhabei war zones to serve, which was quite effective. Later, the Shanghai North Office was established, and the municipal government appointed Huang Ming as the director of the Shanghai North Office. Lu, feeling that his talent was not being fully utilized, became passive and repeatedly submitted his resignation to the municipal government, which was repeatedly retained by the municipal government. The Peiping police also did not accept the local customs and had intentions to leave. Now that the local security has been restored to the state before the January 28th Incident, and the local police force in Shanghai is also sufficient to maintain local security, Captain Lu saw that the time was ripe and led six hundred Peiping policemen to Beijing by train yesterday, heading back to the north via Jinpu. There are still about five hundred Peiping policemen remaining in Shanghai, and it is expected that they will also return to the north one after another after Captain Lu Lu returns to Peiping.

Coming and Going of Japanese Dignitaries 135

Arikawa's Arrival in China: The newly appointed Japanese Ambassador to China, Arikawa Akira, will arrive in Shanghai on September 4th. Japanese Consul Murai told reporters from this newspaper yesterday that Arikawa's sole mission after taking office in China is to demand that the Chinese authorities suppress the anti-Japanese goods movement. Consul Murai had previously protested this matter to Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, but the municipal government has not yet responded. Due to Mayor Wu's request, the content of the Japanese consulate's protest and Consul Murai's conversation with Mayor Yi will not be disclosed. The Japanese side also does not want to exacerbate the situation and therefore does not need to promote it. One point discussed by Mayor Wu and Consul Murai last time has been accepted by the Japanese side, but the Japanese side is not yet satisfied with one other point. As for Ambassador Arikawa's visit to China this time, he is not responsible for negotiating the Northeast Incident, as this issue will be decided after the League of Nations meeting.

Okazaki's Return Home: Shijunsha reports that the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai received a telegram from Arikawa, the newly appointed Japanese Ambassador to China, from Tokyo on the 23rd, stating that he will arrive in China on September 2nd with the newly appointed Director of the Shanghai Special Police Department, Misa, by the Nagasaki Maru from Kobe. The Japanese military and political authorities in Shanghai immediately appointed Okazaki, the Japanese member of the Joint Committee (i.e., the Japanese director of the Municipal Council), to leave Shanghai for Japan on the Japanese mail ship Nagasaki Maru at 9:00 AM this morning to welcome Arikawa. However, although Okazaki's return to Japan is ostensibly to welcome Arikawa, he was actually summoned by the Japanese government to report on the progress of the Joint Committee and to strive for the recovery of the road construction beyond the boundaries and the current situation of goods arriving in Shanghai. It is also heard that when Okazaki returns to Jinjiang at the beginning of next month, in addition to Arikawa and Misa, the newly appointed Consul-General to Shanghai, Ishii, will also come to Shanghai together.

Yano's Journey to Beijing: Since the discovery of the Iron-Blooded Assassination Corps, the Japanese Embassy has held important meetings for days, discussing nothing but the issue of resisting Japanese goods. At 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, Yano Makoto convened an emergency meeting at the embassy office, attended by Chief of Staff Tashiro, Lu Haijun Kitaoka, and military attachés. The main point of discussion was that although a protest had been filed with the municipal government regarding the actions of the Iron-Blooded Assassination Corps, the city government had not strictly prohibited the boycott of Japanese goods. A unanimous decision was made that Deputy Ambassador Yano would go to Beijing immediately to request the National Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to strictly ban the group and to strictly prohibit the boycott of Japanese goods. Otherwise, the Chinese government would be fully responsible if the city's security was endangered in the future. Yano Makoto has scheduled to travel to the capital this morning on the Beijing-Shanghai Army. However, this trip is nominally a visit to important figures in our government in the capacity of the newly appointed Acting Ambassador to China, but it is actually a protest to our government regarding the issue of resisting Japanese goods.

Harada Returns to Changchun: Harada Shunichi, the former high-ranking adviser sent by the pseudo-Manchukuo government, came to Shanghai via Dalian from Changchun by ship. His mission was indeed ordered by the pseudo-government to discuss important matters with the Japanese military and political authorities in Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, he visited various important figures in the Japanese authorities in Shanghai for days. Now that Harada's mission is complete, he returned to Changchun by ship yesterday.

Takeuchi Returns to Japan: Takeuchi, the Japanese Deputy Consul in Shanghai, was ordered last week to come to Shanghai to investigate the recent anti-Japanese goods movement in Shanghai and to prepare for the expansion of the Japanese Police Department. He completed his mission and returned to Japan the day before yesterday (24th).

Sea Vessels Still Suspended Yesterday 139

Hurricane Not Abated

The hurricane in Shanghai has lasted for three days, and the Fujian-Zhejiang sea vessels that have been suspended in Shanghai have not been able to leave, resulting in huge losses. The current situation is as follows:

Hurricane Direction: The hurricane moved from Taipei to the Wenzhou Ocean the day before yesterday and turned towards Fuzhou. According to the report from the Xujiahui Observatory yesterday, the hurricane's trend is still circling over the Wenzhou Ocean. This hurricane is moving very slowly. There are clouds and strong winds and showers in the southern part of the Yangtze River. The hurricane is blowing from Wenzhou towards the west-northwest. There are extremely strong easterly winds and gales in the Yellow Sea, and the climate in the East China Sea is also very bad. There is also sudden rain and gale in the east-southeast.

Three Days of Suspension: The Taikoo's New Beijing and New Ning Shao, which are Shanghai-Ningbo liners, are still docked in Zhenhai yesterday.

Page 14

They have not come to Shanghai yet. The Zhaoshang's Sanbei, which is in Shanghai, and the Ningbo ship believed that the two ships were blocked for two days, causing significant business losses. They had planned to depart yesterday, but the hurricane warning was even worse than the day before yesterday, so they were ordered to continue to stop sailing and simply change to departing on Saturday. Eight of the twelve Ningbo ships this week will be suspended due to the wind.

Obstruction of Entry and Exit: The Guangji, Xinfeng, Guangli, and various Shanghai-Taiwan liners that had departed the day before yesterday encountered a hurricane as soon as they sailed out of Wusong. Mayor Wu Discusses Ways to Remedy the City's Finances 141

It is decided to implement a business tax and increase the land tax

According to the Central News Agency, the city government's budget for this year is short by three million yuan. Secretary-General Yu Hongjun convened a meeting with the heads of the Finance Bureau and other three bureaus, as well as Xu Shengchan, manager of the city bank, the day before yesterday to discuss the issue. A solution was agreed upon, but it has not been announced because it needs the mayor's approval. Yesterday, Mayor Wu told a reporter from the Central News Agency that the specific methods to remedy the situation include implementing a business tax and a land tax, which are still under discussion. The business tax will be levied in accordance with the previously announced regulations. The concession areas must also be implemented at the same time. The method has now been agreed upon with the concession authorities. The collection of land donations is not to increase the burden on the people. The land prices in commercial and residential areas of Nanshi and Zhabei have increased to tens of thousands of taels per mu due to commercial prosperity, while the land donations are still the same as those of rural fields in Zhenru, with only one yuan of grain tax per mu, which is clearly unfair. Therefore, it is planned to estimate the land prices in the above two districts and increase the collection proportionally. The implementation date will be at the end of this year or the beginning of next year.

Borrowed Grain Needs to be Postponed Again 142

For the borrowed grain from Jiangsu Province, 4.5 yuan per stone is still owed. It was previously decided that starting from 1930, 9 jiao would be repaid annually until 1934. However, due to the provincial treasury's deficit, the implementation was postponed. This year's winter grain tax is being collected, and it should have been repaid. However, the Shanghai County Government received instructions from the Jiangsu Finance Department yesterday that, due to the province's finances, following last year's floods and then the Shanghai War, the province's treasury revenue and expenditure have been sharply reduced, and income cannot cover expenses. The budget deficit for this year is quite large. It has been submitted to the provincial government for approval, and all borrowed grain that should be repaid this year will be postponed for another year to ease the financial strain. The county government has received the order and immediately instructed the Finance Bureau to comply.

Fishery Trade Opposes Levying Fishery Tax 143

And requests the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to find a way to save the situation

The Shanghai Fishery Trade Association, with the recent news that the authorities will implement the levy of a fishery tax, yesterday sent a special letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting the government authorities to immediately find a way to save the situation. The original text is recorded as follows: "Respected Sirs, recently, fish merchants from Ningbo and Taizhou have been inquiring with our association, saying that they have recently heard news of a heavy fishery tax being levied. If this is implemented, the fishermen's last hope for survival will be completely deprived. Please help us appeal, etc." Our association believes that fishery trade is closely related, and pays great attention to this matter. Rumors are rampant. On March 28 of last year, the National Government issued an order stating that the fishery industry in our country is declining day by day. If it is not actively promoted and properly protected, it will not be enough to save it and revitalize it. Therefore, the fish tax and fishery tax are all exempted. In the future, no matter what agency, it shall not establish another name to levy this tax, so as to comply with the government's intention to eliminate cumbersome procedures and protect the fishery industry, etc. After the order was received, the fishermen of Jiangsu and Zhejiang were moved to tears, and believed that there was hope. Unexpectedly, after only one year, there was a rumor of the revival of the fishery tax. Alas, our small people are running around telling each other, and we really don't know where to turn for tears. In order to save and revitalize the fishery industry, the National Government specifically exempted the fish tax and fishery tax, and repeatedly stated that no matter what agency in the future, it shall not establish another name to levy this tax. According to our usual reasoning, we thought that with this guarantee, it could be maintained permanently. Now, the decline of the fishery industry is still the same. Can it be said that it has been saved? Can it be said that it has been revitalized? No one can answer this. The government wants to show great faith to the people, or will not change its mind. Only the fishermen are already on the verge of bankruptcy. In addition to the domestic pirates, the dumping of foreign fish is increasing day by day, and they cannot bear to be exploited again. Hearing this rumor, they are extremely alarmed. In addition to sending a telegram to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry to request their assistance, we have sent a special letter to your association, begging you to consider the pain of the fishermen and quickly forward it to save the situation. We are deeply grateful to the public."

The Municipal Government Schedules Arbitration for the Sanyou Factory Labor Dispute 149

The Ministry of Industry Telegraphed the Shanghai Labor Protection Section Chief to Consult on Resolution

Party and Government Agencies to Send Personnel to Persuade the Workers to Eat First Today

According to the Dagong Daily, the Sanyou Factory strike dispute has been decided by the Municipal Government to be submitted to arbitration. The Ministry of Industry specially telegraphed Zhang Tiejun, the Chief of the Labor Protection Section of the Ministry in Shanghai, yesterday, instructing him to consult nearby and jointly seek a solution. The fasting workers are still refusing to eat. Party and government agencies will send personnel today to jointly persuade them to resume eating first and wait for a solution. The details are as follows:

Telegram from the Ministry of Industry: The Ministry of Industry of the National Government telegraphed Zhang Tiejun, Chief of the Labor Protection Section of the Ministry of Industry in Shanghai yesterday, saying, "To Zhang Tiejun, Chief of the Labor Protection Section in Shanghai, recently, we received an urgent letter from the Cotton Textile Industry Workers' Union of the Seventh District of Shanghai, stating that Sanyou Company is delaying the resumption of work, and the workers are desperate for a chance to live. Therefore, Hong Jiaben and 23 others voluntarily went on a hunger strike. Please adopt effective measures to transfer and order an early resolution, and strictly order the capitalists to continue to pay food expenses before the resolution, etc." In addition to telegraphed to the Shanghai Municipal Government, strictly order the capitalists to resume work as soon as possible, and approved outside, the joint telegraph to the Chief of the Section, quickly together with Deputy Director Wang of the Central Committee Wu the Section Chief to consult nearby to resolve the issue to be compassionate to the difficulties of the workers, Ministry of Industry Yang.

Persuade to Eat First: Hong Jiaben and 23 other workers in the factory have been fasting since the 18th, and it has been the eighth day as of yesterday. Those who joined later have also been fasting for five days and nights. During this period, in addition to being force-fed milk once by the General Labor Union, although party and government agencies and the Municipal General Labor Union have repeatedly sent personnel to persuade them to eat, the fasting workers have firmly refused to accept because there is still no hope of a solution. Now the families of the fasting workers have heard the news and have come to Shanghai in large numbers, and the situation is very tragic. If the fasting continues, unfortunate events will inevitably occur. Therefore, Zhu Xuefan, a standing committee member of the General Labor Union, visited Wang Manyun, director of the Civil Training Section of the Municipal Party Department, and Wang Xianqing, director of the Mediation Section of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, yesterday, requesting them to quickly find a way to persuade the workers to eat first and wait for a solution. Directors Wang and Wang also decided to go to the Labor Hospital and Shanghai Hospital today to persuade the workers in writing to resume eating and avoid accidents.

Scheduled Arbitration: The Municipal Government believes that the Sanyou Factory dispute has been mediated repeatedly by the Social Affairs Bureau without success, so it has decided to submit it to arbitration. It has appointed Councilor Luo Panhui as the chairman of the arbitration committee, and has appointed Xu Jiqi as the capitalist member and Zhao Shusheng as the labor member. As for the representative of the Municipal Party Department, it is also heard that Committee Member Lu Jingtulu will attend. Only after the representatives of the special local court and the special first court are appointed can the arbitration begin. However, Councilor Luo believes that the case is extremely urgent, and in order to deal with it quickly, he has decided to convene an arbitration meeting at 2:00 p.m. on the 31st of this month to submit the arbitration.

Relief Meeting: The General Labor Union's Relief Committee for Fasting Workers of Sanyou Factory held its second meeting at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. The attending committee members Ye Xianggao, Li Mengnan, Yu Xianting, Chen Peide, and Tan Honglin decided on the following: (1) Submit to the Municipal Government, allowing the Relief Committee to send representatives to attend the arbitration; (2) Continue to send representatives to persuade the workers to eat first; (3) Order all labor unions to donate money to help as much as possible; (4) Schedule another meeting at 2:00 p.m. on the 27th.

Zhang's Talk: A reporter from the Dagong Daily specially visited Zhang Tiejun, Chief of the Labor Protection Section of the Ministry of Industry, yesterday to ask for his opinion on the Sanyou Factory labor unrest and the handling process. He was kindly received and made a speech saying that since the Sanyou labor unrest occurred, the Ministry of Industry has telegraphed me for detailed investigation. A few days ago, Vice Director Wang Lu of the Central Civil Movement Committee and Section Chief Wu Zhongheng of the Workers' Section came to Shanghai, and the Ministry of Industry telegraphed again to ask us to consult together to resolve the issue. After receiving the order, I have repeatedly consulted with Committee Member Wang and Section Chief Wu. As a result, it is believed that the reasons for the Sanyou Company's capitalists to suspend the factory are not sufficient. The company was founded with very little capital at the beginning, and has expanded year by year to achieve its current scale. Regardless of whether it is purely from dividends or additional capital from foreign shares, at least it is mixed with the blood and sweat of the workers. Now, because of a slight setback, it ignores the livelihood of thousands of workers, which is cruel in terms of facts and human feelings. Now that mediation is hopeless, the government has no choice but to adopt extraordinary means and adopt effective compulsory arbitration methods. Yesterday, I and Section Chief Wu visited Mayor Wu to discuss in detail. A considerable method has now been drafted and can be implemented. Today, I went to the Labor Hospital to see the fasting workers, and witnessed the tragic situation of the fasting workers, and felt that the government could not help but seek a solution quickly.
