Criminal Judgments

Zhou A'wu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of providing premises for opium smoking for profit. Chen Sanlin, Kong Shuntang, Lü A'er, and An Yong'sui are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall each count as one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. Kong Shuntang, Lü A'er, and An Yong'sui are granted a three-year suspended sentence.

Luo De'sheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of providing premises for smoking opium substitutes for profit. Zhang Zheng'rong, Wang Lai'fa, Lu Ji'rong, Gui Sheng, Xu A'bao, and Yu Jia'li are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes. Wang Cai'bao is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of being a recidivist in smoking opium substitutes. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall each count as one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. Lu Ji'rong, Cai Gui'sheng, and Xu A'bao are all granted a two-year suspended sentence.

Wang A'san is fined 200 yuan for possession of opium substitutes. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall count as two yuan of the fine for every one day of detention.

Lu Yunquan is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of providing premises for smoking opium substitutes for profit. Ma Bingzhi is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes. Wu Ziwen is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of being a recidivist in smoking opium substitutes. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall each count as one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. Ma Bingzhi is granted a three-year suspended sentence.

Li Mao'nan is fined 100 yuan for the crime of illegally detaining a close relative. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall count as two yuan of the fine for every one day of detention. The robbery portion of Li Mao'nan is not accepted.

Qian Jin'sheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 120 yuan for the crime of providing premises for opium smoking for profit. Chen Zaixing is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall each count as one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention.

Tang A'san is fined 60 yuan for possession of opium. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall count as two yuan of the fine for every one day of detention.

Zheng Da'min and Zhang Shi'xing are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Zhang A'qing, Xie Yun'sheng, and Chu A'bing are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. Ling Shenqing v. Wu Guoliang for land rental appeal: The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. Ruling: Pudong First Glass Factory v. Xu Weizhang for eviction appeal: The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. Ruling: Zhu Zhiyang v. Xu Dayuan for a debt appeal: The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. Zhang Zhiqing v. Lu Liansheng for a loan dispute: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 160 yuan in silver dollars. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The parties shall each bear their own litigation costs. Xu Bingxiang v. Xinghua Company et al. for a goods dispute: The defendant Xinghua Company shall repay the plaintiff 622.43 yuan in silver dollars. If they are unable to repay, Xieji Chicken and Duck Shop shall be responsible for repayment within the scope of 500 yuan. The defendant Xinghua Company shall bear the litigation costs. Jie Nengsheng v. Du Youji et al. for a loan dispute: The defendant Du Youji shall repay the plaintiff's loan of 170 yuan in silver dollars. If they are unable to repay, Wu Fuji shall be responsible for repayment. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. Wu Yinfu v. Huang Genshu et al. for a debt dispute: The defendant Huang Genshu shall repay the plaintiff 150 yuan in silver, with annual interest at a rate of 2% from October 9th (lunar calendar) of the 16th year of the Republic until the date of execution, but not exceeding the original amount. If Huang Genshu is unable to repay, Huang Shaotang shall be responsible for repayment and may auction the two bungalows and their land located at the Wengjia Shebozi Xuhao in plot 14, group 25 Shangse to recover the debt. The defendant Huang Genshu shall bear the litigation costs.
